                                                                                                Statement of Loans

  The Statement of Loans is divided into two volumes. Each volume is organized by region, and within region by country department and country. The country department and country name are
printed on the lower right corner of each page. The following index provides an easy means to refer to the report. The regional data is followedby the information on loans to IFC and Taiwan,
Province of China. Please note that all questions concerning the contents of this report should be referred to the Loan Accounting and Borrower services Division, Controller's Questions or
changes concerning distrbution should be referred to Mail and Distribution, General Services.

NOTES


1. LOANS ARE MADE (A) TO THE MEMBER, OR (B) TO A POLITICAL SUBDIVISION OR A PRIVATE ENTERPRISE IN THE TERRITORIES
   OF THE MEMBER WITH THE MEMBER'S GUARANTEE. LOANS HAVE ALSO BEEN MADE TO THE INTERNATIONAL FINANCE CORPORATION
   AND TAIWAN, CHINA.


2. AGREEMENTS IN THE TOTAL AMOUNT OF USD         7,022,575,760.00 PROVIDING FOR THESE LOANS HAVE BEEN SIGNED. BUT THE
   LOANS HAVE NOT BECOME EFFECTIVE AND DISBURSEMENTS THERE UNDER DO NOT START UNTIL THE BORROWERS AND GUARNANTORS.
   IF ANY, TAKE CERTAIN ACTIONS AND FURNISH CERTAIN DOCUMENTS TO THE BANK.


3. THIS INCLUDES $0.01 OF EFFECTIVE LOANS WHICH THE BANK HAS AGREED TO SELL. IT ALSO INCLUDES
   THE U.S. DOLLAR EQUIVALENT OF UNDISBURSED CURRENCY COMMITMENTS UNDER CERTAIN DOLLAR EQUIVALENT LOANS MADE TO
   IFC. THESE CURRENCY AMOUNTS HAVE BEEN VALUED WITH THE EXCHANGE RATES OF THE DATE OF THIS STATEMENT OF THE
   UNDISBURSED BALANCE.


4. THE INTEREST RATE WAS NOT FIXED AT THE TIME THE LOAN WAS SIGNED, BUT WAS TO BE DETERMINED SUBSEQUENTLY AS
   PROVIDED IN THE LOAN AGREEMENT.


5. OBLIGATIONS UNDER THESE LOAN AGREEMENTS WERE ASSUMED BY THE LISTED BORROWERS BY SUBSEQUENT LOAN ASSUMPTION
   AGREEMENTS.


6. LOAN NUMBER 472-0 IFC FROM $100,000,000.00, MADE IN 1966, WAS CONSOLIDATED INTO LOANS 650-1 AND 650-2 IFC FOR
  $200,000,000.00.


7. THE SOLD PORTION OF THE LOAN INCLUDES A GRANT PARTICIPATION.


8. CANCELLATIONS INCLUDE TERMINATIONS.


9. INCLUDES EXCHANGE ADJUSTMENT ON DUE THIRD PARTIES.


10. THE BANK HAS APPROVED AND INDICATED ITS WILLINGNESS, SUBJECT TO CERTAIN CONDITIONS, TO EXECUTE THESE LOANS
  AMOUNTING IN TOTAL TO USD        5,698,048,400.00 .


11. NOT APPLICABLE


12. REPRESENTS LOANS MADE AT THE TIME WHEN THE AUTHORITIES ON TAIWAN REPRESENTED CHINA IN THE WORLD BANK. THE
  AUTHORITIES ON TAIWAN HAVE AGREED TO SERVICE THESE DEBTS.


13. THE ORIGINAL PRINCIPAL OF THESE LOANS HAS BEEN REDUCED BY A TOTAL AMOUNT OF $5,374,556,154.60 REPRESENTING
  TRANSFERS TO THE CURRENCY POOLING SYSTEM.


14. THE ORIGINAL PRINCIPAL OF THESE LOANS, TOTALING $5,374,556,154.60 REPRESENTS AMOUNTS PREVIOUSLY COMMITTED
                 INTERNATIONAL BANK FOR RECONSTRUCTION AND DEVELOPMENT                                                 Page: 1,274
                              STATEMENT OF LOANS - May 31, 2016


 UNDER LOANS NEGOTIATED PRIOR TO JULY 1, 1980 BUT TRANSFERRED. AT THE ELECTION OF THE BORROWER, TO THE CURRENCY
 POOLING SYSTEM. THE APPROVAL DATE, THE AGREEMENT DATE AND THE EFFECTIVE DATE THAT APPEAR AGAINST THE
 TRANSFERRED AMOUNTS REPRESENT RESPECTIVELY THE BOARD APPROVAL DATE OF THE ORIGINAL LOAN, THE DATE OF AMENDMENT
 OF THE ORIGINAL LOAN AGREEMENT TO PERMIT THE TRANSFER, AND THE DATE ON WHICH THE AMENDMENT BECAME EFFECTIVE.


15. THE ORIGINAL PRINCIPAL AMOUNT OF THE LOAN IS EXPRESSED IN U.S. DOLLAR EQUIVALENTS. THE LOAN IS TO BE DRAWN DOWN
  IN CURRENCIES TO BE AGREED UPON BETWEEN IBRD AND IFC. THE UNDISBURSED AMOUNT OF THE LOAN REPRESENTS THE
  AGGREGATE U.S. DOLLAR EQUIVALENT OF THE UNDISBURSED CURRENCY AMOUNTS AGREED TO DATE, AT THE EXCHANGE RATES OF
  THOSE CURRENCIES AS OF THE DATE OF THIS STATEMENT, PLUS THE PORTION OF THE ORIGINAL U.S. DOLLAR EQUIVALENNT
  COMMITMENT IN RESPECT OF WHICH THE CURRENCIES OF DRAWNDOWN HAVE NOT BEEN AGREED TO.


16. THE ORIGINAL PRINCIPAL AMOUNT UNDER B LOANS IS SHOWN AT THE RATE OF EXCHANGE APPLICABLE ON THE DATE OF APPROVAL:
  HOWEVER, AMOUNTS DISBURSED ARE QUOTED AT THE MARKET RATE ON THE DATES OF DISBURSEMENT.


17. THESE ARE GUARANTEES AND CONTIGENT OBLIGATION APPROVED UNDER THE CO-FINANCING PROGRAM WITH PRIVATE BANKS
  (B LOANS). THE AMOUNTS SHOWN ARE NOT INCLUDED IN THE TOTAL ORIGINAL PRINCIPAL.


18. THE BORROWER'S OBLIGATION INCLUDES THE AMOUNT OUTSTANDING DUE 3RD PARTY
  AT CURRENT VALUE IN THE AMOUNT OF USD            0.01


19. THE UNDISBURSED, DUE IBRD, LOANS HELD AND BORROWER'S OBLIGATIONS ARE
  VALUED AT THE EXCHANGE RATE APPLICABLE ON THE DATE OF THIS STATEMENT FOR ALL
  LOANS DENOMINATED IN A CURRENCY OTHER THAN US DOLLARS.


20. THIS LOAN HAS BEEN CONVERTED TO SINGLE CURRENCY LOAN (SCL)/SINGLE CURRENCY POOL (SCP) PARTIALLY/FULLY.


21. ACCUMULATED DISBURSEMENTS IN A SEMESTER (DISBURSED AMOUNT) FORM A SUB-LOAN UNDER EACH SCL FIXED RATE LOAN.
  ON THE RATE FIXING DATE, THE DISBURSED AMOUNT IN THAT SEMESTER BEGINS ACCRUING INTEREST AT THE APPLICABLE FIXED
  LENDING RATE, WHICH APPLIES THROUGHOUT THE MATURITY OF THAT PART OF THE LOAN.
  HENCE, THERE IS MORE THAN ONE RATE FOR EACH SCL FIXED RATE LOAN.


22. THOUGH NOT ACTUAL DISBURSEMENTS, THE INFLATION ADJUSTMENT FOR INFLATION-INDEXED LOANS IS PRESENTED FOR
  CONVENIENCE UNDER DISBURSEMENTS.
